 rudki devbhumi haridwar kaa hissaa he or isliye maansaahaari khaanaa rudki ke hostalon main nahin diya jaataa tha, lekin congress kii sarkaar main iaiti rudki main maansaahaari bhojan shuru karvaa diya gaya
 In IIT Roorkee, a mosque for employees was converted into a community mosque
 control sirf iaiti kaa nahin rahaa
 Our sources revealed that since October 2014, non-vegetarian food has started in the hostels of Roorkee but has not been made
 baahar se aata he
 In October 2014, it was the NDA government, not the UPA
 rudki ke hostalon main shaakaahaar kii parampara rahi he
 As far as the mosque is concerned, which comes in the IIT campus, first of all no one is allowed to go to the campus without an IIT sticker, but if someone wants to go to the mosque, then no one is forbidden
 
 
 or masjid iaiti rudki kii property nahin he, vakf kii property he
 In Haridwar, meat and liquor are not allowed within the six km radius of Harki Pauri
 uske baahar in dukaanon ko sarkaar hi license detii he
 Meat and liquor shops are contributing to government revenue as IIT Roorkee exits
 iske baad bhi hamen is mugalate main bhi nahin rahanaa chahie ki sansthaaon kaa raajnneetik istemaal sirf bijepi aresas karti he

 Bardhan's son-in-law Sameer Barua was made director of IIM Ahmedabad
 faikalti member ne samir barua ko doosraa turm diye jane kaa virodh kiya tha
 The author has supported the draft IIM Bill 2015 which will make it difficult for political parties to decide a director or chairman
 draft bill main saaf-saaf likhaa he ki chairman yaa nideshak kii niyukti centre sarkaar karegi
 The Board of Governors shall have nominated members of the Center and the State
 phir bhi orgeniser ne draft bill ko sahi samajha he to us hisaab se gajendra chouhan se lekar un sabhi kaa virodh karnaa chahie jinaki niyukti apatiai main hui he or jinka sambandh bijepi or aresas se rahaa he
 The comments - anagha ghaisas ke pati sangh ke prachaarak rahe hai, unhone pradhanmantri narendra modi ke prachaar ke liye documentry banaai he

 kya vyaapman ghotaale main khulaasa karne vaale kai purv swayamsevak bhi anti hindu bataa diye jaaenge
 i do not know how much can separate the thinking of the organizer and the RSS, but without the consent of the thinking of the RSS, nothing can splash in the organizer
 to kya hoga agar kisi virodh pradarshan ko anti hindu, anti india kah diya jaae
 In Organizer magazine, Sandeep Singh wrote that as soon as the central government appointed Gajendra Chauhan as the director, anti-hindu elements started opposing him because he played the role of Dharmaraj Yudhishthira
 gajendra chouhan ne 150 filmon or 600 se zyaada siriyal main kaam kiye hai
 There is no one like him who opposes BJP, even you are Ananthamurthy
 aap jaanate hai ki kai dinon se pradarshan kar rahe apatai ke chaatro kaa anupam kher, salmaan khan, ranbir kapur, rishi kapur jaise kai kalakaaron ne samarthan kiya he
 Will Anupam Kher now become anti-hindu
 ajay devgan jaise kai kalakaaron ne gajendra chouhan kaa samarthan bhi kiya he to ajay devgan hindu samarthak ho gaye
 Is it a warning that he who opposes will be identified as such
 orgeniser ne likhaa he ki koi dimagi rup se biimaar hi gajendra chouhan kii saakh kaa virodh kar saktaa he
 The author is unable to decide whether Gajendra Chauhan's opponents are anti-hindus or mental patients
 unhen yah samajhnaa chahie ki gajendra ji ne yuddhishthir kaa role kiya tha, ve yuddhishthir nahin hai
 i do not know if Gajendra Chauhan's film Open Window and Jawani Jaanman was religious or not
 maine to dekhi nahin
 The author has made another interesting argument in front of the anti-hindu students that the protesters forget that the beginning of the Indian film industry begins with Raja Harishchandra who was a life-size figure in Hindu and Indian history
 aaj bhi industry kaa sabase bada award raja harishchandra banane vaale dada sahab phalke ke upar hi he
 i can only guess that these students will also face opposition from the film 'raja Harishchandra' and its producer Dada Saheb Phalke
 orgeniser ne neuyork times main chape salil treepathi ke lekh kaa hawala dete hue likhaa he ki you aar ananthamurti kaa bas chalata to bhartiya cinema shatabdi 2055 main manati kyonki you aar ananthamurti ke anusaar bharat kii pehali film raja harishchandra nahin, sathyajith re kii pather panchali he
 If this is true, then how have the authors come to the conclusion that the protesting students will also have the same opinion as Ananthamurthy

 According to the World Health Organization (WHO) report, Delhi ranks 11th in the category of polluted cities
 dilli main pradooshan str kii baat karen to abhi se hi hawa jehar ban chuki he
 Talking about the real time air quality index in Delhi, Anand Vihar recorded the highest pollution level on Tuesday morning
 anand vihaar main piem 2
 a level of 5 where the average was closer to 307 micrograms / cubic meter, which is five times higher than the normal level (60)
 vaise sirf dilli nahin duniya bhar ke kai shahar pradooshan se grasit hai
 The Chinese capital Beijing is also polluted by directing people to stay home
 smog ke chalate vahaan ke nagarikon ko zyaada se zyaada vaqt ghar main rahane ke liye kaha jaataa he
 This instruction is given to citizens due to pollution reaching dangerous levels in the capital

 rajya kii 403 sadasyeey vidhansabha main bijepi-endie ke paas 324 vidhayak hai (unhen kul 325 siton par jeet mili thi, lekin nurpur ke vidhayak kaa nidhan ho chukaa he

 mayawati ko congress ke saat vot or areldi ke ek vot milane kaa bharosa he

 congress kaa aarope tha ki un donon ne bhaajapa ko vot dene ke baad ballat paper dikhaa diya tha

 ek vot kii keemtcross voting sapa-basapa kii raah kaa roda ban saktaa he

 Suddenly, a strong fire broke out from the kitchen of the house and caught 12 people present outside the kitchen
 inamen chaar saal kaa baccha bhi shaamil tha
 Hearing the scream of the injured, the people immediately gathered on the spot and all the injured were admitted to Lord Mahavir Hospital in Pitampura
 fire kii gaadi bhi maukey par pahunch gai, lekin aag failane se pehle hi logon ne us par kaabo paa liya tha
 It is being told that the condition of four people in the injured is critical

 Witnesses say that a small cylinder of gas kept in the kitchen was seeping, but it went unnoticed
 achaanak se gas kahin se aag ke sampark main ai
 After this, a fire broke out, which hit 12 people

 nae draft ke mutabiklokapaub cabinet mantriyon or jajon kaa nilamban nahin kar saktaa

 yani saajha samiti kii pehali baithak main dhak ke vahi teen paat rahe

 jan lokapal bill ko baithak main saamne rakhane ke baad nae draft main kai badlaavon par sahmati bani

 saath hi lokapal ko nyaayadhishon kaa nilamban karne kaa adhikaar bhi naa diya jaae

 baithak main isapar bhi sahmati ban gai ki lokapal ke liye salection kamity main pradhanmantri or netaa vipaksh bhi hon, pehle uparashtrapati or loksabhaa spikar kaa naam tha

 lokapal bill par hui saajha samiti kii baithak ke baad sarkaar kaa rukh sakaaratmak dikhaa

 baithak main sarkaar kii taraf se pranav mukherjee, pi chidambaram, virappa moili, kapil sibbal or salmaan khurshid ne hissaa liya to janata kii taraf se anna hajaare, shantibhushan, santosh hegade, prashanth bhushan or arvind kejariwal bhi baithak main pahunche the

 uskaa naam he 'sonya'
 Sonya of Kalamwadi village does not need to be taken
 wo khud hi doodh ladi gaadi lekar dairy tak jaataa he or phir khaali ken waapas ghar tak le aata he
 Sonya covers a distance of about 3 kilometers 2 times daily
 ek baar subah or phir dusri baar shaam ko
 Sonya's owner Shivaji Salunkhe says that Sonya was born from a cow in her house
 tabhi se wo is kadar ghul mil gaya he ki use haankane kii jarurat hi nahi padati
 According to Salunkhe, he has 4 brothers but his father Sonya is called his 5th son
 salunkhe ke mutabik un kii 10 acre jameen he
 They have a total of 40 animals including cows, buffaloes and bulls
 lekin sonya un sabase hat ke he
 Sonya is 10 years old
 wo aksar use baiylgaadee ke jot kar doodh dairy jaaya karte the
 One day, when the bullock stopped taking the cans of milk on the cart, Sonya left for Derry alone
 uske baad se to ye roj kaa kaam ho gaya
 He takes 200 liters of milk in the dairy himself twice daily
 kalamwari gaanv ke nivasee pratap scindia kaa kahana he sonya ab unke gaanv kii shaan ban gaya he

 khaas baat he ki raste main koi badi car yaa gaadi aa jaati he to sonya khud hi bagal ek taraf ruk jaataa he

 saadhaaran sa bail apane asaadhaaran kartab kii vajah se gaanv kaa celibrity ho gaya he

 dakshin africa ke khilaaf centurian test main bharat kii sharmnaak haar hui he

 team india kii haar kaa sabase bada kaaran bane apana test debyue kar rahe 21 varshiya tej gendbaaj lungi nagidi

 unhone top order main captain viraat kohli or keel rahul ko out kiya saath hi madhya kram main hardik pandya or aar aswin ko pavilion bhej kar dakshin africa kijit kii ibaaratlikh di

 2 over gendbaaji kii jisamen 5 madan over bhi shaamil the

 CA officials left without telling the media and fans

 pehla test brisben main 4-8 disambar ke bich khelaa jayega

 unki jagah pehle test main kohli captaini kaa bhaar sanbhaalenge
